1. Notionã§ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ã‚’ä½œæˆã—ã€ä»¥ä¸‹ã®é …ç›®ã‚’è¨­å®šï¼š

     - Name (title)

     - æ–°ä½æ‰€ (rich text)
     - å¤‰æ›´æ—¥ (date)

   - ç‰©æ•…è€…æƒ…å ±ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹ï¼š

2. Notion APIã‚­ãƒ¼ã®å–å¾—ã¨è¨­å®šï¼š
   - Notionã®é–‹ç™ºè€…è¨­å®šã‹ã‚‰APIã‚­ãƒ¼ã‚’å–å¾—
   - `.env`ãƒ•ã‚¡ã‚¤ãƒ«ã« APIã‚­ãƒ¼ã¨ãƒ‡ãƒ¼ã‚¿ãƒ™ãƒ¼ã‚¹IDã‚’è¨­å®š

3. ãƒ—ãƒ­ã‚¸ã‚§ã‚¯ãƒˆã®ã‚»ãƒƒãƒˆã‚¢ãƒƒãƒ—ï¼š
```bash

```

```javascript
});

const DECEASED_DATABASE_ID = process.env.NOTION_DECEASED_DATABASE_ID;
```

```javascript
    try {
        const { name, era, graduationYear, oldAddress, newAddress, changeDate, remarks } = req.body;

        const response = await notion.pages.create({
            parent: {
                database_id: ADDRESS_DATABASE_ID,
            },
            properties: {
                Name: {
                    title: [
                        {
                            text: {
                                content: name,

                        },

                },

                                content: oldAddress,

                    ],
                },
                "æ–°ä½æ‰€": {
                    rich_text: [
                        {
                            text: {
                                content: newAddress,
                            },
                        },
                    ],
                },
                "å¤‰æ›´æ—¥": {
                    date: {
                        start: changeDate,
                    },
                },
                "å‚™è€ƒ": {
                    rich_text: [
                        {
                            text: {
                                content: remarks || '',
                            },
                        },
                    ],
                },
            },
        });

        res.json({ success: true, message: 'ä½æ‰€å¤‰æ›´ãŒæ­£å¸¸ã«ç™»éŒ²ã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸ' });
    } catch (error) {
        console.error('Error:', error);
        res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãŒç™ºç”Ÿã—ã¾ã—ãŸ' });
    }

```

```javascript
function debounce(func, wait) {
    let timeout;
    return function executedFunction(...args) {
        const later = () => {
            clearTimeout(timeout);
            func(...args);
        };
        clearTimeout(timeout);
        timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
    };
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // è¦ç´ ã®å–å¾—ã‚’æœ€é©åŒ–
    const menuToggle = document.querySelector('.menu-toggle');
    const mainNav = document.querySelector('.main-nav');
    const body = document.body;
    const header = document.querySelector('.header-content');
    const menuItems = document.querySelectorAll('.main-nav li');

    // ãƒ¡ãƒ‹ãƒ¥ãƒ¼é …ç›®ã«ã‚¢ãƒ‹ãƒ¡ãƒ¼ã‚·ãƒ§ãƒ³ç”¨ã®ã‚¤ãƒ³ãƒ‡ãƒƒã‚¯ã‚¹ã‚’è¨­å®š
    menuItems.forEach((item, index) => {
        item.style.setProperty('--i', index);
    });

    // ä»¥ä¸‹ã€æ—¢å­˜ã®ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰...
});

// ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•ã®è¨­å®šã‚’æ›´æ–°

    // ... æ—¢å­˜ã®chartOptionsã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ ...
};

// ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•ã®è¨­å®šã‚’é©ç”¨

charts.forEach(canvas => {
    const chart = Chart.getChart(canvas);
    if (chart) {
        chart.options = { ...chart.options, ...chartOptions };
        chart.update();
    }
});

// ã‚¦ã‚£ãƒ³ãƒ‰ã‚¦ã‚µã‚¤ã‚ºãŒå¤‰æ›´ã•ã‚ŒãŸã¨ãã«ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•ã‚’æ›´æ–°

    charts.forEach(canvas => {
        const chart = Chart.getChart(canvas);
        if (chart) {
            chart.options = { ...chart.options, ...chartOptions };
```

```javascript
// debounceé–¢æ•°ã®å®šç¾©ã®å‰å¾Œã«è¿½åŠ 
console.log('Before debounce definition');
function debounce(func, wait) {
    console.log('Debounce function defined');
    let timeout;
    return function executedFunction(...args) {
        const later = () => {
            clearTimeout(timeout);
            func(...args);
        };
        clearTimeout(timeout);
        timeout = setTimeout(later, wait);
    };
}
console.log('After debounce definition');

// DOMContentLoadedã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆã®ä¸­ã«è¿½åŠ 
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    console.log('DOMContentLoaded event fired');
    
    // Canvasè¦ç´ ã®ç¢ºèª
    const charts = document.querySelectorAll('canvas');
    console.log('Found canvas elements:', charts.length);
    
    // ã‚°ãƒ©ãƒ•é–¢é€£ã‚³ãƒ¼ãƒ‰ã®å®Ÿè¡Œå‰ã«è¿½åŠ 
    console.log('Before chart initialization');
    charts.forEach((canvas, index) => {
        console.log(`Processing canvas ${index}:`, canvas.id);
        const chart = Chart.getChart(canvas);
        console.log(`Chart instance for canvas ${index}:`, chart);
    });
});

// resize ã‚¤ãƒ™ãƒ³ãƒˆãƒªã‚¹ãƒŠãƒ¼ã®å‰ã«è¿½åŠ
```

ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ ã®é€ä¿¡å•é¡Œã‚’è¨ºæ–­ã™ã‚‹ãŸã‚ã«ã€æ®µéšçš„ã«ãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°ã‚’è¡Œã„ã¾ã—ã‚‡ã†ã€‚

1. ã¾ãšã€ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ é€ä¿¡ã®ãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’è¿½åŠ ã—ã¾ã™ï¼š

```javascript
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    console.log('DOM loaded, checking for forms...');
    
    const addressForm = document.getElementById('address-change-form');
    const deceasedForm = document.getElementById('deceased-info-form');
    
    console.log('Address form found:', !!addressForm);
    console.log('Deceased form found:', !!deceasedForm);

    if (addressForm) {
        addressForm.addEventListener('submit', async function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            console.log('Address form submitted');
            
            const formData = {
                name: document.getElementById('name').value,
                era: document.getElementById('era').value,
                graduationYear: document.getElementById('graduation-year').value,
                oldAddress: document.getElementById('old-address').value,
                newAddress: document.getElementById('new-address').value,
                changeDate: document.getElementById('change-date').value,
                remarks: document.getElementById('remarks').value
            };
            
            console.log('Form data:', formData);

            try {
                console.log('Sending request to server...');
                const response = await fetch('http://localhost:3000/api/address-change', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify(formData)
                });
                
                console.log('Server response:', response);
                const data = await response.json();
                console.log('Response data:', data);

                if (data.success) {
                    alert('ä½æ‰€å¤‰æ›´ãŒæ­£å¸¸ã«ç™»éŒ²ã•ã‚Œã¾ã—ãŸ');
                    addressForm.reset();
                } else {
                    alert('ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãŒç™ºç”Ÿã—ã¾ã—ãŸ: ' + data.message);
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Error details:', error);
                alert('é€ä¿¡ä¸­ã«ã‚¨ãƒ©ãƒ¼ãŒç™ºç”Ÿã—ã¾ã—ãŸ: ' + error.message);
            }
        });
    }

    // ç‰©æ•…è€…ãƒ•ã‚©ãƒ¼ãƒ ã‚‚åŒæ§˜ã®ãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’è¿½åŠ 
    if (deceasedForm) {
        // ... åŒæ§˜ã®ãƒ‡ãƒãƒƒã‚°ãƒ­ã‚°ã‚’è¿½åŠ 
    }
});
```
